By wielding such a virtual brush, you can make vastly different marks which normally require switching between many 'brushes' in other programs. The use of GPU makes such a simulation fast enough for real-time interaction, even on a tablet computer.\r\n\r\nFinally, the simulation is paired with a new rendering method that gives you both raster richness and vector-like output up to 12k resolution.
